## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as UnitTest
    participant Handler as SubscribeToRealTimeNotificationHandler
    participant UserDAO as FakeUserDAO
    participant OrgDAO as FakeOrgDAO
    participant RuleDAO as FakeNotificationRuleDAO
    participant Request as FakeRequest

    Test->>UserDAO: construct (persona_id present)
    Test->>OrgDAO: construct (org_fv_id present)
    Test->>RuleDAO: construct
    Test->>Handler: instantiate with DAOs
    Test->>Request: construct (is_valid = true, notification_rule_id = null)
    Test->>Handler: handle(Request)
    Handler->>UserDAO: lookup user by auth0_id
    Handler->>OrgDAO: lookup org by org_id
    alt request.notification_rule_id is null
        Handler->>RuleDAO: create(notification rule)
        RuleDAO-->>Test: assertWasCreated
    else notification_rule_id exists
        Handler->>RuleDAO: update(notification rule)
        RuleDAO-->>Test: assertWasUpdated
    end
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram
    [*] --> ValidRequest
    ValidRequest --> CreatedSubscription : notification_rule_id is null and DAOs valid
    ValidRequest --> UpdatedSubscription : notification_rule_id provided
    ValidRequest --> [*]
    state CreatedSubscription {
        [*] --> RuleCreated
        RuleCreated --> [*]
    }
    state UpdatedSubscription {
        [*] --> RuleUpdated
        RuleUpdated --> [*]
    }
    ValidRequest --> BadRequest : user missing OR org missing OR request invalid
    BadRequest --> [*] : raises BadRequestError
```
